using namespace std;
int main()
{
	int i,n,ar[30];
	int pos,num;
	cout<<"enter the size of array: ";
	cin>>n;
	if(n>30)
		cout<<"out of range!";
	else{
	
		cout<<"enter the elements of array\n";
		for(i=1;i<=n;i++){
			cin>>ar[i];
		}
		for(i=1;i<=n;i++){
			cout<<"ar["<<i<<"]="<<ar[i]<<endl;
		}
		cout<<"enter the number you want to insert:";
		cin>>num;
		cout<<"enter the position: ";
		cin>>pos;
		for (i = n; i >= pos;i--){
		  	ar[i+1] = ar[i];
		    }
		ar[pos] = num;
		n++;
		for(i=1;i<=n;i++){
			cout<<"ar["<<i<<"]="<<ar[i]<<endl;
		}
		}
}

26/08/22, 10:25 pm - +91 6387 438 544: #include <cmath>
#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;


int main() {
    int i,a, max,index;
    cin>>a;
    int arr[a];
    for(i=0;i<a;i++){
        cin>>arr[i];
    }
    max = arr[0];
    for(i=1; i<a; i++){
        if(max < arr[i])
        max = arr[i];
    }
    for(i=a-1; i>=0; i--){
        if(arr[i]==max)
        {
            index = i;
            break;
        }
    }
    cout<<index;
    cout<<endl;

    return 0;
}

    /* Enter your code here. Read input from STDIN. Print output to STDOUT */ 
    void insertElement(char Arr[], int &n, char z, int m) 
    {
    for (int i = n; i > m; --i)
    {
        Arr[i] = Arr[i-1];
    }
    Arr[m] = z;
    ++n;
    }

int main () {
    int n; 
    int s ;
    cin >> s;
    if (s <= 0 || s > 20)
    {
        cout << "Invalid size of array" << endl;
        return 0;
    }
    char Arr[2*s];
    int i = 0;
    do
    {
        cin >> Arr[i];
        ++i;
    }while(Arr[i-1] != '\0');
    n = i-1;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i)
    {
        if (Arr[i] >= 'A' && Arr[i] <= 'Z') 
        {
            insertElement(Arr, n, Arr[i]+32, i+1);
        }
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i)
    {
        cout << Arr[i] << " ";
    }
    return 0;
}

using namespace std;
struct node
{
public:
int data;
node *next;
};
struct node *head=NULL;
void insert(int new_data)
{
struct node *new_node=new node;
new_node->data=new_data;
new_node->next=head;
head=new_node;
}
void display()
{
struct node *ptr;
ptr=head;
while(ptr!=NULL)
{
cout<<2*ptr->data<<endl;
ptr=ptr->next;
}
}
int main()
{
insert(4);
insert(3); insert(2);
insert(4);
insert(1);
cout<<"The linked list is: ";
display();
return 0;
}

2. using namespace std;
int main()
{
    int M;
    cin >> M;
    int a[M];
    for (int i = 0; i < M; i++)
    {
        cin >> a[i];
    }
    int N;
    cin >> N;
    int b[N];
    for (int j = 0; j < N; j++)
    {
        cin >> b[j];
    }
    int final_size = M + N;
    int c[final_size];
    for (int k = 0; k < final_size; k++)
    {
        if (k < M)
        {
            c[k] = a[k];
        }
        else
        {
            c[k] = b[k - M];
        }
    }
    for (int f = 0; f < final_size; f++)
    {
        cout << c[f] << " ";
    }
    return 0;
}

05/09/22, 7:24 pm - +91 72249 72033: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;
struct node
{
public:
    int data;
    node *next;
};
struct node *head = NULL;
void insert(int new_data)
{
    struct node *new_node = new node;
    new_node->data = new_data;
    new_node->next = head;
    head = new_node;
}

int main()
{
    int temp = 0;
    int data;
    do
    {
        cin >> data;
        if (data != -1)
        {
            insert(data);
        }
    } while (data != -1);

    int count = 0;
    struct node *ptr;
    ptr = head;
    while (ptr != NULL)
    {
        if ((ptr->data) % 2 == 0)
        {
            count++;
            temp = 1;
        }
        ptr = ptr->next;
    }
    if (temp != 0)
    {
        cout << count;
    }
    else
    {
        cout << "No even number present";
    }
}

using namespace std;
struct node
{
public:
    int data;
    node *next;
};
struct node *head = NULL;
void insert(int new_data)
{
    struct node *new_node = new node;
    new_node->data = new_data;
    new_node->next = head;
    head = new_node;
}

int main()
{

    cin>>n;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++)
    {
        int age;
        cin>>age;
        insert(age);
    }

    ptr=head;
    int count = 0,temp=0;
    while (ptr != NULL)
    {
        if ((ptr->data) > 18)
        {
            count++;
            temp = 1;
        }
        ptr = ptr->next;
    }
    if (temp != 0)

    }

    {
        cout <<0;
    }

#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
#include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
struct node{
public:
int data;
node *ptr;
};
struct node *head = NULL;
void insert(int new_data)
{
struct node *new_node = new node;
new_node->data = new_data;
new_node->ptr = head;
head = new_node;
}
bool isPalin(){
struct node * slow= head;
stack <int> s;
while(slow != NULL){
int n = slow->data;
int reversed_number=0;
while(n != 0) {
int remainder = n % 10;
reversed_number = reversed_number * 10 + remainder;
n /= 10;
}
s.push(reversed_number);
slow = slow->ptr;
}
while(head != NULL ){
int i=s.top();
s.pop();
if(head -> data != i){
return false;
}
head=head->ptr;
}
return true;
}
int main(){
int n;
cin>>n;
if(n<5 or n>=15){
cout<<"Invalid Input";
return 0;
}
for (int i = 0; i < n; i++){
int num;
cin>>num;
insert(num);
}
int result = isPalin();
if(result == 1)
cout<<"Yes";
else
cout<<"No";
return 0;
}

13/09/22, 11:26 am - Nilesh Tech-a-thon: #include <cmath>
#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;

bool isPerfectSquare(int x)
{
    int s = sqrt(x);
    return (s * s == x);
}

bool isFibonacci(int n){
    return isPerfectSquare(5 * n * n + 4) || isPerfectSquare(5 * n * n - 4);
}

int main() {
    int n;
    cin>>n;
    int arr[n];
    vector<int> idx;
    for(int i=0; i<n; i++){
        cin>>arr[i];
        if(isFibonacci(arr[i])){
            idx.push_back(i);
        }
    }
    for(int i=0; i<n-1; i++){
        arr[idx[idx.size()-1]] = -1;
        idx.pop_back();
        for(int j=0; j<n; j++){
            if(arr[j]==-1)  continue;
            cout<<arr[j]<<" ";
        }
        cout<<endl;
    }
    return 0;
}
